The Council storyline ends with Reed walking away. He does not destroy them. He leaves them to their work and goes home to Sue.

**The Future Foundation (FF #1 vol. 4, 2011).** After Johnny's apparent death in the Negative Zone, Reed reconstitutes the team as the Future Foundation — Franklin, Valeria, the Moloids, Dragon Man, Alex Power, Bentley-23, Artie and Leech. The behavioral significance is that *Reed has chosen succession over solo operation*. He is teaching. He is, in clinical terms, doing what no Council-Reed did: building an environment in which the next generation will *not* repeat his isolation pattern.

He treats Valeria, in particular, as a full intellectual peer from age four onward. The file logs her interactions with him as the most relationally healthy of his life — not because they are warm in conventional terms (they are often acerbic, technical, contested) but because she has from infancy been calibrated to *interrupt his model when it runs without input*. She is, functionally, the daughter version of the spousal interoceptive prosthesis he constructed with Sue. The fact that Reed *engineered the conditions* for this — by treating her as a peer from the beginning, refusing the infantilization that would have rendered her inert — is, in the file's reading, his single most successful long-term reparative project.

**Johnny's return; Reed's quiet weeping (FF #600, 2011).** Recorded for the affect register: Reed, on Johnny's return, weeps in public and does not perform the affect. He does not narrate it. He does not technicalize it. The expression arrives in real time, externally visible. This is the rarest data point in the file's affect archive. It marks the maturation of the channel under sufficient relational scaffolding.

---

## K. Incursions and Secret Wars (2013–2015): The Worst Iteration of the Pattern at the Largest Possible Scale

The Hickman *Avengers* / *New Avengers* run from 2013 onward documents the discovery, by the Illuminati, that parallel Earths are colliding (the "incursions"); each incursion ends a universe unless one of the two Earths is destroyed in time. The Illuminati — Reed central among them — undertake to destroy other Earths to preserve their own.

The pattern: identified. The scale: planetary-to-multiversal. The concealment: from Sue, for years.

The file marks the following:
- Reed is, at every decision point, the *most ethically distressed member of the Illuminati*. T'Challa and Namor are clearer-eyed; Strange is more transactional with the necessary cost; Stark is operating in his own register. Reed is the one who cannot sleep, who builds the antimatter injector and cannot bring himself to use it, who has to be relieved at the trigger.
- Reed conceals the entire operation from Sue. The justification is protection — *if she knew, she would oppose, and the opposition would not change the outcome but would cost her the capacity to function*. This is the Civil War rationalization in larger handwriting. The fact that he has run it twice in less than ten years is the file's strongest evidence that *meta-cognition has not yet translated into behavioral change at the highest stress strata*.
- When Sue learns (and she does, in *Time Runs Out*), the rupture is the deepest of the marriage. She does not file. She tells him, in published dialogue, that she has been *unable to stop noticing* he has been hiding something for years. The file logs this exchange as critical: Sue, the relational prosthesis, has been registering the concealment the whole time. Reed's defense — that he was protecting her — fails on the evidence of her own bandwidth. She did not need protection; she needed *partnership*. He gave the wrong gift.

**The Raft (Secret Wars, 2015).** As the final incursion ends all realities, Reed and a small group escape on a constructed life-raft. He emerges, on the other side of the Battleworld arc, as a *world-builder in the literal sense* — accepting, with full meta-cognitive awareness, the demiurgic role that has been the implicit endpoint of his entire trajectory since FF #1. He spends the post-Battleworld period rebuilding the multiverse with Franklin and Sue at his side.

The file's reading: this is the *resolution* of the middle period, not its continuation. Reed has reached the maximum possible scale of his operational pattern, has done the work, has done it *with his family present rather


## Chronology IV — Recent History & Current State

# Chronology IV — Recent History & Current State

## SUBJECT: RICHARDS, REED — Surveillance Window: post-*Secret Wars* reconstitution through present operational status

---

## 4.1 Re-Entry Phase — The Eight-Year Absence and Its Residue

The operative fact governing every behavior in the current dossier window is this: the subject, his wife, and his two children were *absent from the prime continuity for approximately eight years of in-world and out-of-world time*, during which they traversed the multiverse repairing realities damaged by the incursion event. When Reed Richards returned to Earth, he returned as a man who had spent nearly a decade in the role he had refused at the Council of Reeds — *itinerant cosmic repairman*, severed from the planetary anchor he had previously identified (per the Hickman thesis) as the variable that kept him human.

The reconstitution period must be read against this. He returned with:

- **A fully aged Valeria and Franklin** carrying multiversal experience their pre-absence selves did not have; the parental relationship is now noticeably more peer-adjacent, especially with Valeria. The subject defers to her on theoretical questions with a frequency unobserved in any prior era. This is not deference-as-affection; it is deference-as-empirical-respect, which from Reed is the higher-order affection.
- **An unresolved breach with Ben Grimm**, who had been on Earth all those years marrying and building a life with Alicia Masters. Reed's first instinct was reparative gift-giving (a customized home, technological accommodations); Ben's response was muted gratitude masking a registered grievance. The grievance, behaviorally, is the same one from 1961: *you decided what was good for me without asking*. Reed has not yet directly addressed it. He has built around it.
- **A re-encounter with Johnny Storm**, who in the absence had been the most decompensated member of the surviving group — substance use, public spectacle, depressive presentation, an ill-considered marriage. Reed's reintegration with Johnny is paternal in the specific manner of a man who knows he is too late to have prevented the damage and is now performing maintenance.
- **A marriage that survived the *Secret Wars* concealment** — the most severe breach in its history — by the mechanism of forced co-presence during the multiversal repair work. Sue's pattern of forgiveness here is not absolution; it is the operational truce of two people who chose to keep building. The fault line documented in §3 is *not closed*. It is dormant.

## 4.2 The Yancy Street Re-Establishment

Surveillance places the family residence, for the bulk of the post-return window, at the *Four Yancy Street* address — a deliberate downsizing from the Baxter Building era. The choice is behaviorally significant: a townhouse footprint over a skyscraper-lab footprint imposes proximity, reduces the available physical infrastructure for the lab-as-flight-response, and forces the subject into the same kitchen as his wife and children at predictable intervals. Reed selected the site; Sue ratified it. Read this as a deliberate environmental engineering of his own behavior — the subject *building a building that makes it harder to do the thing he reliably does under stress*.

Observed daily routine, current window:

- **04:30–05:30** — Wake; this is unchanged across sixty years of record. Coffee, prepared by hand, black. He brews enough for Sue, who does not rise until ~07:00, in an insulated carafe — a small standing tenderness ritual of the type the subject performs in *absence* of the recipient, where the affective register does not need to be managed in real time.
- **05:30–08:00** — Lab work, basement level. Door open per house rule (Sue-imposed, post-return). Compliance variable.
- **08:00–08:45** — Family breakfast when achievable. Surveillance indicates achievement rate ~60–70%, a marked improvement over the pre-*Civil War* baseline of perhaps 20–30%. Failure mode is no longer disappearance; failure mode is *physical presence with cognitive absence*, which Sue now names aloud across the table — a verbal cue ("Reed — *here*") to which the subject responds with measurable latency improvement over time.
- **Workday** — variable; school runs (Valeria insists, despite being theoretically capable of teleporting herself; this is a relational ritual she protects); Future Foundation work; consulting; emergencies.
- **18:30–20:00** — Dinner block, protected. This is new behavior. Across the Lee/Kirby through Hickman eras dinner was sacrificial; in the current window it is treated as load-bearing.
- **22:00–02:00** — Second work shift, lab. Sleep is still pathologically curtailed (cf. §2); the subject sleeps approximately 4–4.5 hours per 24-hour cycle on a maintained schedule, with occasional 48–72 hour work jags during crisis events. This has not improved and likely will not.

The Yancy Street residence is, in surveillance terms, *the most relationally aware physical environment the subject has ever inhabited*, and his behavior within it reflects an asymptotic approach to — not arrival at — domestic normality.

## 4.3 Operational Posture — Reduced Public Footprint

The current window shows a marked withdrawal from the Avengers / Illuminati / cape-political register that defined the Millar–Hickman decade. The subject has *not* re-joined the Illuminati framework even where it has been reconstituted; surveillance reads this as deliberate. The Illuminati was the institutional embodiment of his worst structural tendency — like-minded peers ratifying decisions he had already made (§4, escalation ladder, high-stress band). His refusal to re-enter it is one of the cleanest pieces of behavioral evidence in the current window that meta-cognition has gained operational traction.

He has, by contrast, expanded:

- **Domestic-scale scientific consulting** — quiet work for civilian agencies, often pro bono, on infrastructure problems (water, energy, atmospheric remediation). Pattern is *un-glamorous applied engineering*, almost ostentatiously so. The subject is performing a corrective on his prior reputation as a cosmic generalist who did not see street level.
- **Mentorship** — the Future Foundation framework has been informally reconstituted on a smaller scale, with Valeria as effective co-director. The subject treats this as succession planning, which it is, and as therapy, which it also is.
- **Direct Ben Grimm collaboration** — current run shows the cure-attempts have been formally suspended at Grimm's request; Reed's surrogate behavior is now *engineering accommodations for Ben's life as it is*, which is a categorical maturation: from reparative compulsion (undo the harm) to reparative companionship (sit with the harm). This is the single most significant clinical development in the current window.

## 4.4 The Doom Vector — Current Status

Victor Von Doom has cycled through, in recent canon, an "Infamous Iron Man" reformist arc, a return to villainy, and most recently the *One World Under Doom* configuration in which Doom assumes a sovereign global posture. Reed's behavioral response across these cycles is the most diagnostically rich vein in the current dossier window.

When Doom was reformist, Reed was *not relieved*. Surveillance recorded increased anxiety, increased lab time, and explicit verbal expressions to Sue (per witnessed dialogue) of distrust of the appearance. The clinical read: Reed cannot psychologically accommodate a *good Doom*, because a good Doom would invalidate the Doom-as-externalized-accusation function (§3, self-concept) that organizes a portion of his own self-policing. He *needs* Doom to be Doom in order to know that he himself is not Doom.

When Doom returned to overt antagonism, Reed's affect normalized. This is informative.

Under the current sovereign-Doom configuration, the subject is operating in a constrained adversarial mode — *strategic patience*, model-building, refusal of premature escalation. He has been observed declining direct confrontation invitations from other parties (including Avengers-adjacent groupings) on the explicit reasoning that Doom under conditions of public legitimacy is a *political* problem, not a punch-out problem. This is correct analysis and also a recognizable defense — the same expected-value reasoning that produced the *Civil War* error, now applied with the chastening of that error in memory. Sue is read into every step. The unilateralism is, for now, suppressed.

## 4.5 The Children — Current Configuration

**Valeria Richards.** Now operating as a near-peer scientific collaborator. Surveillance places her in the lab with her father an estimated 15–20 hours per week. The relational mode is *Socratic with affection underneath* — they argue mechanism, they argue ethics, she is the only person in the subject's life who can checkmate him in his own discipline and the only person who routinely does so. The clinical significance: Valeria functions as the *continuous reality-testing on his blind spots* identified in §4 prognosis. When she names a Doom-style overreach in his reasoning, he stops. He does not stop for anyone else with that reliability, including Sue.

**Franklin Richards.** Reality-warping power has been depleted/restructured in recent canon; Franklin is currently operating closer to the human baseline than at any prior point in his life, with corresponding identity reconfiguration. Reed's behavior here is the most affectively legible of the current window: he is *visibly* relieved that Franklin's powers no longer mark him as cosmic-scale-fragile, and *visibly* grieving the loss for Franklin himself, and unable to fully express either. Surveillance has recorded multiple long quiet sits between father and son in which nothing diagnostically significant is said and the subject's expressive output appears minimal — but the recurrence of the behavior, freely chosen, is the data. He shows up. He sits. He does not fix. This is, for him, advanced practice.

The Annihilus / Franklin-coma debt (§1, 1973) is being amortized in real time through these sits. Reed has never verbally re-litigated the event with Franklin; the repair is being conducted in the affective register Reed has historically failed to access. That he is accessing it now, however imperfectly, is the second major clinical development of the current window.

## 4.6 The Marriage — Current Operational State

Susan Storm Richards remains the load-bearing element. Current-window behavior:

- **Public.** They are observed walking with deliberate physical contact (her arm through his) at a frequency higher than any prior era. Read as both genuine and as performance to themselves — a daily re-ratification of choice.
- **Private.** Sue runs an explicit verbal disclosure protocol on him post-*Secret Wars*: standing nightly check-ins, framed casually but structurally non-optional, in which the subject is required to state aloud what he is currently working on, who knows, and whether anyone he loves would object if they knew. Compliance is high. Surveillance assesses this as the operationalization of "you decided for me, again" — Sue has built an instrument that makes that specific failure mode harder to execute.
- **Sexual / affective.** Tenderness markers are at career-high frequency. The subject initiates physical reassurance (hand on her back, forehead-touch) at rates not seen in earlier dossier windows. This is consistent with the maturation pattern: the channel has widened, not because the underlying interoceptive architecture has changed, but because he has learned compensatory output protocols.

The structural fault line documented in §4 — *forced choice between global objective function and one specific intimate* — has not been re-tested at *Secret Wars* magnitude in the current window. Until it is, the dormancy is provisional.

## 4.7 Somatic Status — Current

- **Stretching as discharge** persists and is at higher observed frequency in the current window than prior eras, likely as a function of more time in observable domestic space. The fingers-elongating-across-the-console tell remains pathognomonic.
- **Aging arrest** continues; the subject appears mid-40s. Ben Grimm appears his calendar age. Surveillance has recorded the subject's micro-expressions on observation of Ben at rest; the data is consistent with sustained grief he does not name.
- **Sleep debt** chronic, stable, untreated.
- **No substance use.** Caffeine intake elevated. No other intoxicants. Pattern unchanged across the entire dossier.
- **Injury record, current window** — multiple minor combat injuries metabolized rapidly via tissue plasticity; no chronic sequelae of record. The subject has stopped reporting injuries to Sue in real time; she discovers them by inspection. This is a minor concealment behavior of the type the disclosure protocol is designed to surface, and represents the residual stub of the larger pattern.

## 4.8 Cognitive / Meta-Cognitive Status — Current

The most significant longitudinal change is meta-cognitive. The subject now *names* his patterns in conversation, occasionally with self-deprecation, occasionally with visible discomfort. Recorded verbal acknowledgments in the current window include:

- Direct reference, in family settings, to the *Civil War*–era reasoning as having been wrong on grounds that *were available to him at the time and that he chose not to weigh*. This is a categorical shift from the prior pattern of defending the math.
- Spontaneous use of the word "sorry" toward Ben Grimm at a frequency surveillance has not previously documented across sixty years of record. Most instances are unprompted, and most are about small things (an interruption, a forgotten promise), which is structurally interesting — the subject appears to be *training the affective channel on low-stakes reps* before approaching the high-stakes apology that remains, after sixty years, unspoken.
- Stated recognition, in dialogue with Valeria, that *he himself is the kind of variable that has to be watched*. This is the Hickman thesis internalized as conscious self-monitoring rather than left as authorial framing.

## 4.9 Where He Is, Now

He is at Yancy Street most nights. He is in the lab most hours. He is with his wife at dinner more often than not. He is sitting quietly with his son on a couch with a frequency that would have been inconceivable to the man who put Franklin in a coma in 1973. He is arguing tensor calculus with his daughter who is correct slightly more often than he wishes she were. He is building things for Ben that do not pretend to undo what was done. He is watching Doom hold a throne and *not* mobilizing alone. He is sleeping four hours. He is brewing his wife's coffee before she wakes.

He is, in clinical terms, the best operational version of himself the longitudinal record has documented. The engine described in §1 — *optimize the global objective function, accept local relational damage, perform extended reparative labor* — is still the engine. It has not been replaced. It has been *governed*: by an environmental design (the smaller residence), an interpersonal instrument (Sue's disclosure protocol), a peer reality-test (Valeria), a reframed reparative target (Ben as he is, not Ben as Reed wishes to make him), and a hard-won meta-cognition that finally names the pattern aloud.

The prognosis from §4 holds without revision. Excellent for sustained pro-social functioning. Guarded for recurrence of unilateral high-stakes concealment under sufficient pressure — and the current window has not yet, in this subject's terms, *applied sufficient pressure*. The Doom configuration may yet supply it. Surveillance recommends continued longitudinal observation with particular attention to any reduction in the nightly disclosure protocol's frequency, any return of the Illuminati-pattern peer-ratification behavior, and any sustained increase in lab-isolation hours coincident with new cosmic-scale threat data — these three indicators, in combination, would constitute early warning of the pattern's reactivation.

He has not become a different man. He has become a man who knows what kind of man he is, married to a woman who has built a house and a marriage that make it harder for him to be the worst version of that. It is the most that can be asked of a subject with this neurocognitive architecture, this trauma history, and this magnitude of capacity. On the available evidence, he is meeting the ask.

— END SECTION IV —


## Medical History

# MEDICAL HISTORY — SUBJECT: RICHARDS, REED

*File section M. Compiled from longitudinal observation, published medical references in the case corpus 1961–present, and inference from somatic behavior. Where direct clinical documentation is unavailable (the subject's own physician of record is, in most eras, himself), entries are reconstructed from observed behavior, depicted injury, and the engineering of treatment apparatus he has built for his own use.*

---

## M.1 — CONSTITUTIONAL BASELINE (PRE-INDEX, ca. 1930s–early 1960s)

**Childhood.** The biographical record gives a tall, narrow, undersized-for-age child who hit puberty late and never fully thickened. Vision myopic from early adolescence; the iconic temple-graying (first depicted as a sharply demarcated bilateral streak by *FF* #4) is recorded across nearly every era, suggesting either premature focal canities of early onset or, on the more speculative read, a phenotypic marker of the systemizing neurotype the family clearly carries. Photographs in retrospective panels (*FF* #197, Byrne's #271) show the streaks present in late adolescence, before any cosmic exposure — they are constitutional, not radiation-induced, despite the convenient post-hoc symbolism.

**Hospitalizations, pre-flight.** None of record beyond routine pediatric. A subject who was bookish, indoor, non-athletic, and chronically under-slept from approximately age twelve onward — the under-sleep beginning when he discovered he could compress an eight-hour adult workday into the hours between his mother's death and dawn, and never afterward unlearning the habit.

**Maternal death.** Mother (Evelyn) dies during Reed's early adolescence in most tellings; cause variously rendered but consistent with sudden cardiac or cerebrovascular event. The medical detail he carries forward is *the unpreparedness* — there was no period of decline he could model, no warning he could have engineered around. Subsequent behavior under any acute medical threat to Sue or the children reads as overcorrection against this single un-modelable loss.

**Paternal medical history.** Nathaniel Richards: longevity exceptional, traverses centuries via timestream, returns visibly aged but cognitively intact (*FF* #272–273). Reed thus has, in his only available genetic comparand, evidence of constitutional longevity and resistance to neurocognitive decline — a fact he has almost certainly run heritability calculations on and almost certainly never spoken aloud.

**Substance baseline.** Tobacco: the early Lee/Kirby pipe — recurrent across the first six years of the run — is the only depicted recreational substance use in the entire corpus. It is quietly dropped by the late sixties and never returns. The behavioral inference is not anti-smoking moralism but rather *removal of a variable*: oral fixation that interfered with sustained close-work was abandoned the moment its utility curve inverted. Alcohol: trace, ceremonial, never to intoxication across sixty years of published observation. No depicted recreational drug use, ever. Caffeine: heavy, sustained, lifelong — coffee is the only consumable he is repeatedly shown reaching for without looking, the only compound whose absence produces visible degradation in his task-performance.

---

## M.2 — THE INDEX EVENT (ca. age early-30s; *Fantastic Four* #1, 1961)

**Exposure.** Whole-body cosmic-ray bombardment, unshielded, in upper-atmosphere experimental craft. Estimated dose: incalculable by any terrestrial dosimetry; sufficient to produce permanent genetic, cellular, and structural reorganization in four simultaneously exposed individuals with four divergent phenotypic outcomes — itself a finding that should have killed the field of radiation biology and birthed a new one.

**Acute presentation.** Crash survival; ambulation within hours; phenotypic onset within the same day. Reed's specific presentation: elastic deformation of all tissues, retention of form-memory, full conscious control of extension to ranges later documented exceeding 1,500 feet linear and substantial volumetric variability (sphericalization, lamination to film-thinness, vector-controlled multi-limb branching). No loss of proprioception. No loss of fine motor control at any extension within the tested envelope.

**Acute psychological correlate.** The behavioral record from the immediate post-flight panels is recognizably an acute stress response: hyperarousal, decision-flooding, premature commitment to a unifying narrative ("we have a responsibility…"). The narrative he commits to within hours of the crash — *we owe the world for this* — is the load-bearing organizing belief of his remaining life, and it is, clinically, a stress-formed cognitive structure that was never subsequently revisited under non-stress conditions. He never gave himself the option to grieve the body he lost.

**Latent psychological correlate.** Survivor guilt, specifically Ben-directed, immediate and lifelong. (Treated in §M.10.)

---

## M.3 — THE CHRONIC CONDITION ("ELASTICITY") — SOMATIC PROFILE

**Tissue behavior.** Every layer — epidermis, dermis, fascia, muscle, viscera, vasculature, neural tissue, bone — participates in the deformation. The bone behavior is the singular medical anomaly: voluntary plasticity in a tissue that in every other human is rigid by design. Inference: the cosmic-ray reorganization replaced or supplemented the standard mineralized matrix with a substrate that retains tensile load while permitting reversible elongation. No published assay; the subject has reportedly declined to biopsy himself on the grounds that any sample large enough to be diagnostic would be larger than he is willing to lose, and any sample small enough to spare would tell him nothing he doesn't already infer from in-vivo behavior. (This is the only recorded instance in the file of Reed declining an experiment on grounds of personal cost.)

**Proprioception.** Intact and, by inference, *expanded* — he tracks the position of body segments at distances and configurations no human map of the body schema was designed for. The cortical remapping required is presumably continuous and unconscious; no evidence of failure modes (he does not "lose" a hand the way an amputee loses a phantom).

**Interoception.** This is the clinically significant finding and the one most directly relevant to §3 of the analytic basis. A body whose every organ is under voluntary topological control is a body in which the *involuntary* signals — heart-rate spike, gut-clench, throat-tightening, the visceral substrate of named emotion — are either dampened, overwritten, or filtered through a layer of conscious modulation before reaching awareness. The Mul and Butera findings on interoceptive attenuation as the mediator of emotional-empathy latency in systemizing neurotypes apply here with unusual literalness: Reed's interoceptive bandwidth is not metaphorically reduced, it is plausibly *mechanically* reduced by the substrate of his own physiology. He feels in arrears in part because the bodily channel by which feeling reaches consciousness in real time is, in him, an instrument he is always already playing.

**Pain.** No chronic pain syndrome of record. Acute pain present and appropriate (depicted reliably during injury, e.g., the Annihilus assaults, the Onslaught absorption sequence, multiple Doom-mediated wounds). Notable absence: he does not complain of stretching-discomfort even under sustained extremes — suggesting either a high threshold, an analgesic adaptation, or a stoic suppression that decades of family observation should have noticed had it been suppression. Best read: genuine adaptation.

**Aging.** Per Hickman's exposition and Slott-era reaffirmation, the cosmic-ray-induced cellular plasticity carries an incidental life-extension effect. Reed is, on the clock, decades older than he presents. Sue likely shares this; Johnny is depicted with similar deceleration; Ben's case is confounded by the rocky integument. The psychic load of this is rarely externalized but inferable: he is watching the world he was trained into recede, and he is watching Ben suffer in a body that did not get the same gift.

**Form-default.** He returns, at rest, to the same somatic baseline he had pre-flight, with the temple streaks and the angular face. The retention of a *default* shape in a body capable of any shape is itself a clinical curiosity: he could present, voluntarily, as anyone. He does not. The persistence of the default is identity-preservation expressed through morphology — he is unwilling to give up the body his wife married.

**Stretching as discharge.** Repeatedly depicted, across every era: under cognitive load or emotional pressure, fingers extend across consoles, neck cranes toward problems, an arm reaches across a room rather than the body moving toward what it wants. This is, behaviorally, an unconscious externalized fidget — the elastic equivalent of leg-bouncing — and the only consistently visible somatic readout of his internal state. Trained observers (Sue, primarily; Valeria, learning) use it diagnostically.

---

## M.4 — INJURIES (PARTIAL CATALOG, MOST CLINICALLY INSTRUCTIVE)

**Mechanical trauma.** Lacerations, blunt-force, ballistic, energy-weapon, environmental (vacuum, pressure, thermal) — all attested, all survived, most with rapid recovery. The elastic substrate appears to confer significant resistance to penetrating and crushing injury (force dispersed across deformable tissue) but reduced resistance to focused energy, particularly heat, which can locally exceed the substrate's plasticity envelope and produce burn equivalents. The Annihilus arc (*FF* #140–141) shows tissue burns consistent with this vulnerability.

**Energy / radiation, repeat exposures.** Multiple, including but not limited to Negative Zone exposures (chronic dimensional radiation, ill-characterized), Cosmic Cube proximity, Power Cosmic transfer events, and direct contact with Galactus-class energies during various crises. The cumulative dosimetry is unmeasurable; no malignancy of record, which itself suggests that whatever the cosmic-ray reorganization did to his cellular regulation, it included an oncologic suppression effect. He has not, to public knowledge, ever screened himself for it. He is afraid of the answer in a way he is not afraid of most answers.

**Neurological assaults.** Hate-Monger manipulation (early Lee/Kirby); Psycho-Man emotional inversion (Byrne); Onslaught absorption and dissolution (1996); telepathic intrusions of various kinds across the corpus. The Psycho-Man event is the most clinically significant because it produced, briefly, *uninhibited Reed* — affect on full display, rage and grief and want unmediated — and his subsequent behavior shows that he found the experience not liberating but mortifying. The defense structure was not just a habit; it was a load-bearing wall, and he has been reluctant ever since to discover what is on the other side of it.

**Possession / displacement events.** Multiple body-share or consciousness-displacement incidents (Doom body-swap arcs, various cosmic events). No persistent dissociative sequelae of record, which is itself unusual given the frequency; the systemizing neurotype's strong sense of cognitive continuity appears to function as a dissociation-resistant anchor.

**Onslaught (1996).** Functional death and reconstitution; "Heroes Reborn" pocket-universe interval; return. The depicted post-return behavior — withdrawal, irritability when separated specifically from Sue, hypervigilance toward family location — is consistent with sub-threshold post-traumatic adjustment, never formally addressed.

**Civil War / post-Registration era.** No major somatic injury; significant psychological wounding (§M.10). The somatic correlate is the period of weight loss and visibly degraded grooming depicted in *Civil War: The Confession* and surrounding issues — the body announcing what the mouth would not.

**Secret Wars / Battleworld (2015).** Prolonged operation as world-engineer at the boundary of demiurgic function. No clear somatic injury but the post-event behavior is consistent with an extended dissociative-grandiose state followed by reintegration; the closest the file has to a documented manic-equivalent, etiologically attributable to the role rather than to constitutional mood pathology.

---

## M.5 — SURGERIES AND VOLUNTARY MODIFICATIONS

**Conventional surgical record.** Negligible. The elastic substrate renders most surgical indications moot: he can route around tissue damage, has redundant pathways for most functions, and recovers from injuries that would require surgical reconstruction in a baseline human via what appears to be voluntary remodeling.

**Devices.** A short, mostly classified inventory of self-designed monitoring and modulation apparatus (a wrist-worn vitals telemetry he wears under the uniform during high-load operations; a sleep-debt monitor he reliably ignores; an early-generation cardiac event detector built after the Annihilus arc and never publicly disclosed). He is his own clinician of record and his own most-ignored patient.

**The Council of Reeds procedure — DECLINED.** This is the single most diagnostically important *non-event* in his medical file. Offered the surgical-or-equivalent excision of his attachment circuitry ("the selfish gene" in the council's idiom — functionally, the part of him that prefers his family to the project of solving everything), he declined. He looked at the multiverse's collected evidence that nearly every other Reed had accepted, observed what those Reeds had become, and refused. This is, in clinical terms, *insight*: the recognition that the part of him most often experienced as a liability is in fact load-bearing, and that its removal would produce competence without conscience. It is also the single clearest piece of evidence against any narcissistic-spectrum reading of the subject.

---

## M.6 — REPRODUCTIVE / FAMILY-MEDICAL HISTORY

**First pregnancy (Franklin).** Complicated by residual cosmic radiation in Sue's tissues; emergency intervention required (the Annihilus arc, *FF* #140–141, with the Negative Zone retrieval of the Cosmic Control Rod for Sue's stabilization). The infant carried mutagenic load of unprecedented scale, ultimately manifesting as reality-warping capacity. Reed's behavior throughout: engineering response, suppression of affect, sustained refusal to address the prospect of loss until the medical crisis was technically resolved. Sue's later articulation, repeatedly across writers: *you were not with me, you were solving me*.

**Second pregnancy (originally lost; "Valeria").** Stillbirth, with residual cosmic-radiation etiology implicated. Reed's documented response: rebuild. He does not grieve openly in the record; he begins the project that eventually, via Doom's mediated intervention, becomes the living Valeria of the current run. The mediated resurrection is itself a medical-ethical singularity (he allowed his historical rival to deliver his daughter because the outcome math dominated the relational cost) and a behavior pattern in concentrated form.

**Franklin's neutralization.** Reed strips the Power Cosmic from Franklin and induces a protective coma (*FF* #141) to prevent reality-scale catastrophe. This is, in the medical record, *a parent performing an invasive neurological intervention on his own child under a utilitarian rationale*. It is the most important single data point about how Reed metabolizes the conflict between intimate love and global stakes. The marriage nearly ends; the calculus, he maintains across decades of subsequent reflection, was correct; he does not appear to believe he should have done it differently and also does not appear to have ever stopped paying for it internally.

**Sexual / partnered health.** Long-term monogamy, stable, by all available evidence satisfying for both partners through several decades, with the periodic ruptures attributable to the documented unilateralism rather than to anything sexual or physiologically partner-mediated.

---

## M.7 — SLEEP

The most consistently abused physiological system. Multi-day work jags are normalized across every era; coffee load is heroic; family-imposed sleep hygiene (Sue, increasingly Valeria) is the only effective intervention. Behavioral correlates of acute sleep debt in the subject: latency in social response increases, didactic verbosity rises, the unconscious-stretching tic intensifies and propagates (he begins to occupy more volume), and decision-making shifts toward unilateralism — *because consensus-building is slow and he no longer has the affective bandwidth to tolerate slowness*. The Civil War and Secret Wars concealment behaviors both occur against backgrounds of documented sustained sleep deprivation; the file would be incomplete without naming sleep debt as a precondition of his worst decisions.

---

## M.8 — NUTRITION, ACTIVITY, BASIC SOMATIC MAINTENANCE

**Nutrition.** Erratic. Missed meals are routine; Sue's documented historical labor includes physical interruption of work to ensure caloric intake. He eats fast, without attention, and prefers food that does not require utensil-management — the hands are tools and remain on task. No documented food sensitivities. No depicted disordered-eating cognitions; the under-eating is task-displacement, not body-image driven.

**Activity.** Not athletic by conventional measure. The elastic substrate permits adequate baseline conditioning through normal field operations; he has never been depicted in deliberate exercise of record. The body is, for him, instrument — maintained adequately, not cultivated.

**Hygiene and grooming.** Maintained to a consistent professional standard during stable periods; visibly degrades in episodes of acute crisis (the post-Civil War depictions are the clearest). The temple streaks remain, the lab coat remains, the angular jaw remains — the deliberate visual signature is preserved through every transformation because the *image of Reed Richards* is one of the few things the man permits himself to curate.

---

## M.9 — SUBSTANCE USE — DEFINITIVE STATEMENT

No drug use of record outside the brief early-era pipe. No alcohol abuse. No prescription dependence. No documented self-medication. The clinical reading is not virtue but neurotype: a subject who experiences his cognition as identity-constitutive will not voluntarily impair it, and a subject with attenuated interoception is poorly served by substances whose effect is mediated through bodily sensation he is partly closed to. He is, pharmacologically, a clean signal. Caffeine alone exempted.

---

## M.10 — THE PSYCHOLOGICAL FREIGHT OF THE MEDICAL RECORD

A medical history is, in this file, also a history of how a man metabolizes injury into structure. The pattern is consistent across sixty years and worth naming explicitly.

*The index event* he metabolized by accepting the cosmic-ray reorganization as his permanent condition and refusing — across multiple available cures, including the Wizard's, Doom's at various points, and his own occasional successes for the others — to revert. The elasticity is penance worn as physiology. He could, plausibly, fix himself first; he has cured Ben (briefly) before he has cured himself, every single time.

*The Ben injury* he metabolizes by chronic reparative labor: the cure-attempts that span the entire run, the modulator devices, the Negative Zone work, the Future Foundation as in part a continuation of the apology, and — quietly — the absence of any cure-attempt he has not first cleared with Ben himself in the modern era, because the original sin was unilateral consent and he has finally learned. The Mul/Butera framework matters here: he feels the guilt fully, on a long fuse; the channel through which the feeling reaches action is engineering, because that is the channel his neurology has wired open.

*The Franklin coma* he metabolizes by the unusual gentleness with both children in the subsequent decades, the reaction-formation overcorrection most visible with Valeria. He has not, on the record, ever apologized to Franklin in explicit terms for #141; he has spent the rest of Franklin's life trying to be the father whose hand on his son's head means safety rather than diagnosis.

*The Valeria loss-and-recovery* he metabolizes by treating the recovered daughter as a full intellectual peer from precocious age, granting her access to systems and decisions a more conventional parent would withhold. The behavioral logic: *I almost did not have you; I will not also fail to see you*.

*The Civil War / Secret Wars wounds* — psychological injuries with no clean somatic correlate — he metabolizes by the documented meta-cognitive improvement of the Slott-era reintegration: naming the pattern, narrating it aloud, allowing Sue and Valeria to interrupt it earlier in its arc. The pattern persists; the latency between onset and self-recognition has measurably shortened.

*The decelerated aging* he metabolizes by not discussing it. The file contains no published instance of Reed acknowledging that he will likely outlive Ben in conventional biological terms, despite ample opportunity. This is, in a man whose defining trait is the refusal to leave any problem unmodeled, a striking and instructive silence. Some calculations he does not run.

---

## M.11 — CURRENT STATUS AND PROGNOSIS

A subject in his constitutional sixties-by-the-calendar presenting as a man in late prime, with full retention of cognitive function, intact elastic substrate, no chronic disease of record, no substance burden, chronic untreated sleep debt, attenuated interoception with the relational consequences documented in §3 and reaffirmed throughout this section, and a load of unprocessed historical injury — the Grimm injury, the Franklin intervention, the Valeria loss, the Civil War error — that he carries by working, by staying, and by becoming, slowly, the father his father was not and the husband his thirty-year-old self could not yet be.

The body will outlast most of the people he loves. He has not yet, on the record, permitted himself to know this.

— END SECTION M —


## Somatic Atlas

# SOMATIC ATLAS — SUBJECT: RICHARDS, REED

*File segment 04 of the longitudinal dossier. Cross-reference §2 (Medical) and §3 (Psychological). All observations triangulated from sixty-plus years of published behavioral record and inferentially extended to the granular scale a total-surveillance file would require.*

---

## 1. THE PROBLEM OF READING THIS BODY

Before any catalog: a methodological note. The subject's tissues are under partial voluntary topological control. This means standard surveillance baselining — pulse-at-throat, micro-tremor of the hand, dilation of the nostril, postural sway — is corrupted at the source. He can, and on the published record sometimes does, *iron out a tell*. Hands that would tremble are lengthened a quarter-inch and the tremor dissipates into the new compliance. A jaw that would clench can be widened by half a millimeter to release the pressure. A blush distributes across more surface area and reads as paler.

Therefore: the tells he *cannot* suppress, or does not notice in time to suppress, are evidentially weighted higher than the absence of tells he can. The body that obeys cognition is loudest precisely where cognition was looking elsewhere.

---

## 2. STANDING FORM, GAIT, AND BASELINE POSTURE

**Resting height:** approximately 6'1" when held at the human baseline he calls "neutral." He drifts. End-of-day measurements would be lower by as much as half an inch — not from spinal compression but from inattentive slackening of the connective matrix; he must consciously *hold* the standard height. The drift is unconscious and reliable.

**Posture, calm:** shoulders carried high and slightly forward, head canted four to six degrees forward of vertical — the posture of a man whose center of attention is always one focal length out in front of him. Weight slightly on the heels when listening, slightly on the balls of the feet when about to speak. No military squareness; the posture is *attentive scholar*, not *officer*.

**Posture, in lab:** collapses progressively into a quarter-circle hunch over the workbench. He will not notice that his lumbar spine has elongated to accommodate a stool that is too low rather than adjust the stool. Hours-thirty into a problem he is often perched with feet *flat on the floor* and torso *bent at thirty degrees over the bench* with no visible spinal curve — the silhouette of an instrument lamp.

**Posture, with Sue present:** corrects within ninety seconds of her entering the room. Shoulders drop, head levels. This correction is automatic and likely unconscious; he does not appear to register that he is doing it.

**Posture, with Doom in the room:** spine locks. Height settles precisely at standard. Hands still. He will not give Doom the satisfaction of a slouching opponent.

**Posture, with Ben:** softens at the shoulders, opens at the chest. The body that does not relax around most people relaxes around Grimm. He often, without naming it, positions himself half a step closer to Ben than social distance would predict.

**Gait, calm:** long-strided, slightly loose at the knee, hands clasped behind the back or in lab-coat pockets. Approximately 110 paces per minute on flat ground. No arm swing to speak of; arms are storage, not pendulums.

**Gait, urgent:** does not run if he can stretch. The published record is consistent: under time pressure he will *elongate a leg* across an obstacle, *throw an arm* across a room, *project the upper body* through a door before the legs follow. Running, when it happens, is mechanically poor — he is not an athlete and never trained as one.

**Gait, distracted:** drifts left. Across long corridors he will end pressed to the left-hand wall without noticing. Sue has been recorded steering him by the elbow on instinct in such corridors.

**Stair behavior:** ascends two at a time when alone or with peers; one at a time, slowly, with children. Descends always one at a time, hand on the rail — a small caution he never articulates.

---

## 3. THE HANDS

The hands are the primary surveillance surface. They are where his cognition leaks.

**Resting position, calm:** loosely interlaced at sternum height when seated; clasped at the small of the back when standing and listening; one folded over the wrist of the other when standing and being addressed by a superior in expertise (rare; Doom does not count; T'Challa does, on certain matters).

**The stretch-fidget — the master tell.** When the mind is engaged on a problem and the body is unattended, the fingers elongate. Not dramatically; one to three inches, gradually, over the course of a thought. This is the most reliable indicator of cognitive engagement available. The lengthened finger may then:
- tap a surface in a four-beat pattern (the pattern is consistent across decades; an inferential 1-3-2-4 rhythm, not a 1-2-3-4)
- thread itself around a pen or a stylus, sometimes twice
- reach for an object across the desk without the rest of the arm following — the hand simply *arrives*
- coil around the opposite wrist as a self-soothe, the gesture children make with their own hair

He does not notice he is doing this. Sue, Ben, Johnny, and Valeria all notice. Valeria, on the published record, will sometimes silently uncoil his fingers from her own wrist when he has done it without realizing.

**Stretch-fidget under stress:** the elongation increases in *amplitude* and *speed*. Fingers will reach two or three feet without the arm moving. The thumb will lap the index finger entirely. If he catches himself, he retracts in a single quick motion and tucks the hands away — pockets, behind the back, under the table. The tuck-away is itself a tell: he has just realized he was readable.

**Stretch-fidget under threat to family:** stops entirely. The hands become rigidly the size and shape they began as. He is now using cognitive control to suppress the discharge channel because he needs every bit of executive function for the problem. Absence of fidget in a Reed who has been fidgeting is therefore a *more* alarming sign than the fidget itself.

**Writing hand:** ambidextrous in practice but right-dominant by habit. Holds a pen close to the nib, grip soft. Handwriting is small, dense, and right-leaning, with mathematical notation interspersed mid-sentence. Crosses out rather than erases. The crossings are single horizontal strokes, never scribbled — even his deletions are legible.

**Tool handling:** astonishingly delicate. He will pick up a screwdriver with two fingers and a thumb, the grip a surgeon's. Soldering iron held farther back than safety would recommend, because his hand can simply withdraw out of the path of any spit. He has burned himself perhaps a dozen times in recorded canon; he winces, lengthens the affected tissue to dissipate the local heat, and continues.

**Handshake:** initiates with the right, web-to-web, grip moderate, two pumps, release. Does not adjust pressure for the other party's grip; this has been read as arrogance and is in fact inattention. With strangers his palm is dry. With Ben, his hand will sometimes lengthen mid-shake to clap the upper arm — a gesture that began as compensation for Ben's size and became affection.

---

## 4. THE FACE

**Resting facial set:** neutral-to-mild-frown. The corners of the mouth are slightly down at baseline; this is structural, not affective. People misread it as displeasure.

**The temple-grey.** The signature white at the temples is documented from early adulthood and has not advanced significantly across decades. Whether this is somatic stability from the cosmic-ray-mediated cellular plasticity or a stress marker that arrived early and stayed, the published record does not adjudicate. The grey runs in two flares that widen perceptibly when he has been working three or more consecutive days without proper sleep — possibly an artifact of sebum and pallor distribution rather than actual hair change, but observable.

**The eyebrow.** Left brow lifts approximately one to three millimeters when he encounters data he did not predict. This is the single most useful real-time tell available; it precedes verbal response by roughly four hundred milliseconds and is *not* under suppression because he does not know he does it. Sue knows. Valeria knows. Doom probably knows.

**Both brows together:** lift when confronting elegance — a proof, an organism's morphology, a child's drawing. Often accompanied by a slow exhale through the nose.

**Brows down and inward:** ethical distress. The face he made at the Negative Zone prison the first time he walked its corridors; the face he makes when one of his solutions has killed someone.

**The eyes.** Hazel, with greater pigmentation toward the iris periphery. Eye contact is *durational and unblinking*, often uncomfortably so, when he is interested in what someone is saying — he forgets to blink during cognitive engagement. Blink rate at rest is normal (15–20/min); during deep thought it drops to as low as 3–5/min, producing the characteristic *staring* affect. He will not maintain eye contact during emotional conversations; the gaze drifts to a point past the interlocutor's left ear. This is not avoidance of the person; it is recruitment of the visual field for affective bandwidth that his face cannot otherwise spare.

**Tear behavior.** He cries rarely and slowly. The tear, when it comes, is delayed — sometimes hours after the precipitating event, when he is alone or with Sue. Onset is heralded by a long, slow exhale and a hand drawn down the lower face from nose to chin. He does not sob. The shoulders do not move. The body that contains him does not give him the courtesy of catharsis; the grief simply leaks.

**Smile, social:** symmetric, brief, eyes uninvolved. Polite-conference-smile. Held for the duration of a handshake or photograph and released.

**Smile, genuine:** crooked, slightly higher on the left, with crow's-feet engagement and an audible small exhale through the nose. Reserved for Sue, the children, Ben (rarer), Johnny (rarer still — their dynamic is gentle exasperation more than warmth), and certain elegant solutions. The genuine smile is often *delayed* — he registers the cause, then smiles a beat late.

**Smile, with Franklin or Valeria:** the only smile that reaches both the orbicularis oculi and the underlying breath rhythm. He breathes differently around his children.

**Jaw, calm:** soft. Lips slightly parted.

**Jaw, working a problem:** clenched at the masseter, visible. Sometimes the lower jaw will project a millimeter or two forward — a mandibular adjustment that, given his physiology, may be voluntary or involuntary and is functionally a fidget.

**Jaw, restraining anger at Doom:** locked. The masseter is the loudest muscle in his face under those circumstances and the one tell he cannot dissolve into elastic compliance, because the anger itself is what is producing the tension and the anger is the thing he is hiding from himself first.

**The mouth in deep thought:** the lower lip is drawn inward and held by the upper teeth. Released when speech begins. He does not chew the lip; it is contained, not gnawed.

**Speech-prefatory tell:** a quarter-second of breath drawn through the nose before he begins to speak in any register more formal than conversational. The longer the breath, the more carefully he is choosing what to say. A very long breath — two full seconds — precedes ethical disagreement with someone he loves.

**Vocal patterns.** Baseline mid-baritone, articulation precise without affectation, sentence rhythm slightly stilted by mid-sentence parentheticals and qualifications. Speaks more quickly when explaining something he finds beautiful; speaks more *slowly* when explaining something to a child or to a layperson, with no condescension in the slowing — it is rate-matching, not patronage. Voice drops in volume and pitch when speaking to Sue privately, by approximately a tone. Loses fluency under emotional pressure: word-finding pauses lengthen, sentences are abandoned mid-clause and restarted with technical substitutions for the affective word he could not produce. *"I — when you — what I am attempting to indicate is —"* is the structural form of his attempts at apology.

---

## 5. GROOMING, DRESS, AND THE MAINTENANCE OF SURFACE

**Hair:** combed back from a high left part, held in place by water more often than product; on long lab jags the part disintegrates and the hair falls forward across the brow, which he pushes back with the wrist of whichever hand is less occupied. The wrist-push to the brow is itself a fidget; it appears even when the hair is in fact still in place.

**Shaving:** daily by morning ritual; under sleep debt, the shave is missed and he will arrive at breakfast with a day's growth visible. Sue does not comment on this; Valeria does, mildly. The beard, when it grows in over a multi-day jag, is patchy and largely along the jawline rather than the cheek — a structural feature that has remained stable across the published record.

**Nails:** short, clean, square-filed. He files them himself, weekly. Under deep work jags, the nails reach lengths he does not notice until they catch on a sleeve, at which point he files them in five minutes at the bench.

**Bathing:** showers in approximately four minutes; he does not luxuriate. The shower is for thinking; the published record (Waid, Slott) shows him emerging mid-thought with a towel and walking to a notebook before drying.

**Dress, working:** trousers and a button-down with the sleeves rolled to mid-forearm; over this, depending on era, the FF uniform (which is unstable-molecule fabric responsive to his deformation and therefore not a constraint) or a lab coat. The lab coat collects ink stains at the right breast pocket where pens leak. He notices and replaces the coat approximately quarterly.

**Dress, formal:** dark suit, white shirt, dark tie of plain weave. He owns approximately three of these and rotates them without distinction. Does not enjoy formal dress and tolerates it for press and diplomacy.

**Dress, domestic:** soft trousers, a long-sleeved shirt — always long-sleeved, regardless of season; he is mildly defensive about the fact that his bare arms can be unsettling to others and probably to himself.

**Footwear:** the same model of plain leather shoe for decades; replaced as worn. He does not have opinions about shoes.

**Glasses:** sometimes worn for reading in older-era depictions; cosmetic or genuine refractive correction is ambiguous. Holds them at the temple to remove; folds them with one hand and sets them down with the lenses up.

---

## 6. EATING

**Mealtime, baseline:** three meals when family ritual is enforced; one or two when not. He does not feel hunger reliably. Sue has been depicted bringing food to the lab; he eats it without comment, often without looking at it.

**Speed:** moderate-to-fast. Does not linger over food unless conversation has captured him.

**Utensil grip:** correct continental form. Cuts food into uniform pieces before beginning to eat — a small ordering compulsion, mild OCPD-flavored, not pathological.

**Food preferences:** indifferent. Has no recorded strong likes or dislikes. Coffee, black, in volume — the one consistent consumable across every era. The mug is held in both hands when he is listening, in one hand at the rim when he is talking.

**Family meal behavior:** physically present, cognitively variable. He will be drawn into the conversation by direct address. Sue will sometimes touch his forearm to bring him back; the touch produces a half-second blink-and-resettle that is the somatic signature of recall to the moment.

**Refusal cues:** when distressed he stops eating before he stops working. A plate of food untouched at his elbow for an hour is a more reliable distress indicator than anything he will say aloud.

**Hydration:** poor. He will go six to eight hours without water during a work jag. Sue and, increasingly, Valeria, supply it; he accepts without comment.

---

## 7. SLEEP

**Architecture, baseline:** insufficient. Estimated five to six hours when undisturbed, with frequent two-to-three-hour nights during a problem. Polyphasic tendencies during cosmic-scale crises (Galactus, incursions): twenty- to forty-minute naps at the bench, head on forearm or face flat against the workbench surface, body lengthened slightly to redistribute pressure.

**Sleep posture, with Sue:** on his side, facing her, one arm extended under the pillow toward her — sometimes literally extended, his hand resting on her shoulder from across the bed without his arm appearing to span the distance. This is the most intimate of the unconscious stretches.

**Sleep posture, alone:** on his back, arms at the sides, body straight. The posture of a man laid out.

**Sleep onset latency:** poor. He lies awake working problems in his head. Sue has been depicted reading aloud to him to disengage his cognition long enough to permit sleep onset.

**Dreams:** documented as content-rich, often problem-solving. Has woken with solutions. Also documented (Byrne, Hickman): recurrent dream imagery around the test flight, Ben's transformation, Franklin in the coma. Wakes from these without crying out; sits up slowly, lengthens his neck to look at Sue, lowers it, gets up to work.

**Snoring:** none on the published record. Plausible inference: he adjusts his airway in sleep without waking.

**Bed-leaving behavior:** quiet. Does not wake Sue. Will sometimes leave a hand or foot connected to her side of the bed by elongation while the rest of him is in the lab — a tether he is not always aware he has extended.

---

## 8. SEXUAL AND INTIMATE BEHAVIOR

**General orientation of the record:** sustained monogamous marriage of decades' duration, two children, no canonical infidelity. The intimacy is therefore long, private, and inferred.

**Touch, public:** restrained. Hand at Sue's lower back when guiding her through a doorway; brief kiss on the temple when leaving for a mission; her hand in his when they are seated together. He does not perform intimacy for audiences.

**Touch, private:** more abundant on the published record than the public restraint would suggest. He reaches for her when she enters a room, often without looking up. The reach is sometimes literal — an elongated finger touching her wrist before his eyes have left the page.

**Holding behavior:** when she is upset, he wraps. Arms can encircle her twice if necessary. The wrap is enclosing rather than constricting; she has been depicted leaning into it and being held until the breath settles. He will not speak during the wrap unless asked.

**Kissing:** initiated softly, with a hand at the jaw or temple. Brief in public; longer in private. The published record shows post-separation reunions (after Heroes Reborn, after Secret Wars) initiated by him crossing a room to her without speaking and kissing her forehead before the mouth — the forehead is, in his somatic grammar, the gesture of *I have returned*.

**Arousal tells, inferred:** breathing slows and deepens; eye contact lengthens; the speech-prefatory breath disappears because he is not preparing speech.

**Post-intimacy behavior:** he stays. He does not get up to work. This is one of the few categories of time in which the published record shows him capable of remaining bodily present and cognitively quiet for an extended interval. Sue has commented on it.

**Affective availability with children:** physically affectionate within constraint. Will carry a small child on his hip; will let a sleeping toddler be draped across his chest while he reads. The elongation here is intentional and gentle — a longer arm to cradle, a flatter chest to lay a head on. He has been depicted forming a literal hammock of his own torso for an infant Franklin.

**Affective availability with Valeria, specifically:** he sits down to her eye level rather than bending. He listens to her with the same unblinking attention he gives a peer's proof. This is reaction-formation against the Annihilus pattern and it is the gentlest he has ever been documented being.

---

## 9. MICROBEHAVIOR INVENTORY — UNCONSCIOUS

A non-exhaustive catalog of micro-patterns produced without the subject's awareness:

- **The 1-3-2-4 finger tap.** Right hand, on any hard surface. Tempo varies with cognitive load. Indexes active problem-solving.
- **The wrist-coil.** Index finger of one hand wrapped once around the wrist of the other. Self-soothe; appears under mild relational stress.
- **The brow-push.** Wrist of working hand drawn across the forehead, regardless of hair position. Frequency increases with sleep debt.
- **The neck-elongation.** Toward any unexpected sound or unsolved problem. He extends the neck before turning the head, sometimes by three to six inches. He does not notice; observers do.
- **The bench-lean.** Torso bent thirty degrees over a workbench with no spinal curve. Held for hours.
- **The Sue-orientation.** Within ninety seconds of Sue's entry to a room, his posture corrects and his head turns toward her location even when she is silent. He does not know he tracks her.
- **The Ben-proximity.** Half a step closer to Grimm than to anyone else in the configuration.
- **The Doom-stillness.** Total cessation of fidget in Doom's presence. The stillest he ever is.
- **The lab-coat pocket retreat.** Hands tucked away after a stretch-fidget has been noticed; meta-cognitive marker of being-seen.
- **The four-hundred-millisecond brow.** Left brow lift preceding verbalized surprise.
- **The mid-sentence breath.** Nasal inhalation before consequential speech.
- **The post-loss exhale.** Long slow exhale through the nose, hand down the lower face, hours after the precipitating event.
- **The forehead kiss on return.** Reserved for reunions after separation of meaningful duration.

---

## 10. STATE-DEPENDENT SUMMARY MATRIX

**Calm, alone in lab:** elongated fingers; bench-lean; low blink rate; lengthened neck toward the problem; speech to himself in low murmur; coffee held in one hand at the rim. Body distributed across the workspace, occupying more cubic volume than his nominal mass would imply.

**Calm, with family:** posture corrected; fidget suppressed and replaced by small gestures of orientation toward Sue and the children; genuine smile available; speech rate-matched; eye contact softer and shorter than baseline; capable of remaining bodily still on a couch for the length of a film, though cognition will drift.

**Mild stress:** verbosity up; jargon up; fidget-amplitude up; sleep curtailment beginning; coffee intake up; meals missed; hair displacement from the part.

**Moderate stress:** retreat to lab; jaw clench; tear-leak hours after the precipitating event; speech-prefatory breath lengthens; Sue-orientation persists but he does not act on it; children come to him at the bench and he does not redirect them, which is itself a sign — he is too engaged to manage their access.

**High stress (Civil War / Secret Wars regime):** fidget *suppressed* — the fingers do not lengthen because cognitive control is total. Posture rigid. Speech clipped. Sleep almost absent. Eats standing. The unilateral concealment pattern operationalizes; he begins to make decisions without consulting Sue. The body is gathered, tightened, and quiet, which on this subject is a worse sign than


## Attachment & Relational Patterns

# ATTACHMENT & RELATIONAL PATTERNS

## Subject: RICHARDS, REED — Relational Architecture, Longitudinal Mapping

---

## I. ATTACHMENT CLASSIFICATION

**Working classification: Earned-secure, anxious-preoccupied undertow, avoidant under load.**

The subject does not fit cleanly into a single Bowlby/Ainsworth/Main category, which is itself diagnostically informative — sixty years of behavioral record describe a man who has *worked his way into security* from an insecure substrate, and whose acquired stability holds at baseline but decompensates predictably under specific stressor classes. The pattern is what attachment researchers (Main, Hesse, Roisman) call *earned-secure*: an adult whose childhood would have predicted insecure attachment but who has, through sustained corrective relational experience (the marriage; the chosen family; the children), achieved functional security. The corrective relationship is identifiable, dated, and named: Susan Storm, from approximately 1961 onward.

The undertow is the persistent residue. When the operational stakes pass a threshold — civilizational, multiversal, existential to intimates — the subject regresses to an avoidant defense (concealment, unilateral action, work-flight) layered over anxious-preoccupied content (the underlying fear is *losing the people I love by failing to protect them sufficiently*). The avoidance is the *strategy*; the preoccupation is the *fuel*. This is why his unilateralism reads as both cold and desperate at once.

---

## II. ORIGINS

The attachment substrate is laid down by three structuring facts from the pre-flight biography, repeatedly returned to across authorial regimes:

**1. Maternal loss in childhood.** The mother (variously named, generally Evelyn) dies when the subject is young. The loss is recorded as decorous rather than dramatized — which is itself the point. The household response to maternal death is, on the canon record, more work, more books, more silent dinners. The subject learns that *grief is metabolized privately, through cognition*. There is no available script for vocalized mourning.

**2. Paternal abandonment-into-project.** Nathaniel Richards — brilliant, distracted, then literally vanished into the timestream (Byrne, *FF* #271–273) — leaves. The leaving is *for a project*. This is the most consequential single etiological fact in the file. The child internalizes a model in which *the most important adult disappears into work, and the disappearance is the proof of the work's importance*. He will, as an adult, both rage against this template (by *staying*, structurally, in the marriage and household) and reproduce it (by *vanishing into the lab during the very crises his presence is most required*). The partial inheritance is the diagnostic signature.

**3. Intellectual hot-housing as proxy affection.** Love in the natal family is transmitted through *recognition of intellect*. Reading lists, problem sets, the murmured "good" after a correct derivation. This conditions a lifelong equation: *to be loved is to be cognitively seen; to love is to teach*. The didactic register he defaults to with intimates — exhaustively documented from Lee/Kirby forward — is not condescension; it is, in his internal economy, an act of affection. This is also why he is most fluent with Valeria: she returns the register, and the loop closes.

These three facts compose the substrate. Onto them is grafted the index trauma of the flight (§I of the master workup), which establishes the operational rule: *my judgment, when it errs, disfigures the people I love most*. That rule then competes for the rest of his life with the equally strong rule he learned at Reed Sr.'s knee: *trust the model*.

---

## III. THE BONDING SEQUENCE — HOW HE FORMS ATTACHMENTS

Reed's bonding pattern is unusually slow at onset, unusually durable at maintenance, and unusually difficult to terminate. The phases are observable:

**Phase 1 — Cognitive recognition.** The candidate must be *legible to him* on a dimension he respects. With Ben Grimm at State University (the Lee/Kirby/Byrne shared backstory), the recognition was Ben's *physical competence and moral steadiness* — categories Reed lacked and needed. With Sue, initially, it was social fluency and aesthetic presence; later, and more durably, it became her *intuitive social cognition*, which he correctly identified as a faculty he did not possess and required. With Johnny, it was *the adolescent he was implicitly entrusted with*. With Doom, it was *peer-level cognitive threat*, which is a bond of a different valence but identifiably the same recognition mechanism.

**Phase 2 — Conferral of access.** Once recognized, the candidate is admitted to a sphere — the workshop, the lab, the operational councils. Reed marks bond not through verbal declaration but through *granting unsupervised proximity to his ongoing work*. To be allowed in the lab while he is mid-problem is, in his economy, an intimacy gesture. Sue, Ben, Johnny, Valeria, Franklin, and the Future Foundation children all have this access. Tony Stark has it intermittently. T'Challa has it conditionally. Doom is denied it and resents the denial.

**Phase 3 — Reparative obligation.** Once bonded, the subject incurs what is best described as an *unilateral covenantal duty* toward the bonded party. The duty is permanent, asymmetric, and not contingent on the bonded party's behavior. This is most starkly visible with Ben — sixty years of cure attempts conducted regardless of Ben's stated preferences, regardless of Ben's repeated requests to be *let alone about it*, regardless of the cosmic-scale evidence that the cure does not stick. Reed cannot stop because *stopping would be the renunciation of bond*. The same engine runs the marriage during its worst stretches (post-Civil War, post-Secret Wars he conducts *years* of reparative behavior toward Sue), and it runs the relationship with Franklin after the Annihilus depowering.

**Phase 4 — Structural permanence.** The bond is, once formed, effectively unrescindable from his side. He does not leave. He may be left — Sue has filed for divorce, walked out, separated more than once — but he does not initiate dissolution. The behavioral evidence across six decades shows zero instances of Reed terminating a primary attachment by his own choice. This is the *staying* he has built against the paternal template, and it is the single most ethically durable thing about him.

---

## IV. DISTRUST — HIS THRESHOLDS AND HIS BLIND SPOTS

Reed's distrust mechanism is *cognitive before affective*, which produces both characteristic strengths and characteristic failures.

**He trusts on evidence, not on signal.** He is poor at reading the affective microsignals — facial tension, vocal hesitation, the catch in a breath — that would alert a more interoceptively-fluent partner to deception or distress. The Byrne run's most damning sequence is precisely this: he does not register that *the woman in his bed is not his wife* during the Malice / Psycho-Man arc. The interoceptive deficit (Mul et al., 2018; Butera et al., 2022) cuts both inward — he cannot read his own bodily signals fast — and outward, into the reading of others' embodied affective states. He compensates by *trusting the people who have passed the cognitive-recognition test* and by *trusting the model of them he has built*, which means a sufficiently sophisticated substitution can fool him for unconscionable stretches.

**He distrusts institutions reflexively, individuals slowly.** Reed will spend forty issues skeptical of the U.S. government, S.H.I.E.L.D., the U.N. — anything bureaucratic he reads as a poorly-specified optimization process — while extending unwarranted operational trust to specific persons inside those institutions because *the person passed his test*. Civil War is the apotheosis: he distrusted unregulated superhuman activity (the institutional read) and trusted Tony Stark and his own model (the personal read) far past the point where evidence justified either.

**His blind spots are predictable.** He under-distrusts: (a) peer-level intellects who pass the cognitive-recognition gate (this is how Doom has hurt him most), (b) his own predictive models when the math is hard enough to feel virtuous, (c) any framing in which concealment can be re-coded as protection. He over-distrusts: (a) emotional appeals unaccompanied by evidence, which read to him as manipulation even when they are not, (b) his own affective reactions, which arrive late and which he discounts because of their lateness.

---

## V. BETRAYAL — THE SIGNATURE PATTERN

Reed does not betray in the ordinary sense. He does not lie for advantage, take what is not his, exploit, abandon, or deceive for self-interest. His betrayals are of a single specific type, and the type recurs with such regularity across the corpus that it can be named as the diagnostic pattern of his life:

**The Consent Bypass under Conditions of High Predicted Catastrophe.**

The structure is invariant:
1. He identifies a catastrophic outcome via modeling.
2. He identifies that one or more intimates, if consulted, will not consent to the action required to avert it.
3. He concludes that consultation is therefore an unaffordable luxury.
4. He acts unilaterally and, typically, conceals the action.
5. The catastrophe is averted or mitigated; the intimates discover the concealment.
6. The wound to the relationship is structural and named explicitly by the wounded party: *you decided for me.*

The instances are catalogued in §I of the workup but the pattern bears restating relationally: the test flight (he overrode Ben's stated objection on shielding); the Annihilus depowering of Franklin (he acted before Sue could veto); the cloning of Thor / Project 42 (he acted in concealment from Sue, Ben, Johnny); the Illuminati incursion lifeboats (he concealed from Sue for *years* on Hickman's record). Each instance is, ethically, the *same act*. The bypassed party is, with significant overlap, the *same set of people*.

What distinguishes Reed from the ordinary betrayer is that he *registers each instance as a betrayal*, processes the resulting injury as legitimate, and engages in extended sincere reparative labor. The pattern is not denied. It is, in his frame, *the price he pays for being correct on the math*, and he believes — wrongly, by the relational evidence — that the people he loves will eventually come to see it the same way. They never quite do. He keeps trying.

---

## VI. REPAIR — HOW HE PUTS IT BACK TOGETHER

Reed's repair behavior is one of the most distinctive things about him and is, on the long record, *effective*, which is why his marriage has survived events that would have ended weaker pairings several times over.

**Acknowledgment, slow.** The first phase is *not* immediate apology. The first phase is *cognitive metabolization* — usually in lab seclusion — during which he builds an internal model of the harm done. This phase appears, to the wounded party, as continued avoidance, which compounds the original injury. Sue has, on multiple occasions, had to walk into the lab and demand the metabolization happen in her presence. He is teachable on this point and has, post-Secret Wars, demonstrably shortened the lag.

**Acknowledgment, total.** Once he arrives, his acknowledgment is unusually complete. He does not minimize, does not blame-shift, does not negotiate the scope of the harm. *The Confession* (post-Civil War) is the cleanest specimen — a fully accepted admission that he was wrong, with the math shown. He owns errors with the same rigor he owns proofs.

**Reparative labor, indefinite.** The post-acknowledgment phase is where he excels and where his attachment style is most clearly *earned-secure with sublimative engineering*. He builds. He builds toward the wounded party, in their idiom. For Ben: cure attempts, prosthetics, a customized Quinjet, the consideration shown by remembering Ben's poker night and not scheduling experiments over it. For Sue: trips, *real* leaves of absence (rare but documented), the conscious downshift in didactic register, the Future Foundation as a household structure that makes her labor visible and shared. For Franklin and Valeria: presence, increasingly. The labor is open-ended. He does not consider a debt closed because he does not believe debts of this class *can* be closed.

**The structural limit of his repair.** He cannot, by the architecture of his own cognition, *guarantee non-recurrence*. He knows this. The wounded parties know this. The marriage proceeds on the implicit understanding that the pattern will recur and that the repair, when it does, will be sincere. This is a mature accommodation by all parties and it is, in clinical terms, the achieved compromise of an *earned-secure dyad whose insecure member has named the insecurity*.

---

## VII. INTIMACY — THE PHENOMENOLOGY

**Physical intimacy.** Sparsely documented across the corpus (genre constraint) but consistently warm where shown.
